Sampling for Pharmaceutical Water, Steam, and Process Gases

醫藥級水、蒸汽與製程氣體取樣指南

本章目錄 / Table of Contents

Core Insight of This Chapter | 本章核心觀念

The fundamental challenge of pharmaceutical utility sampling is that what you measure at one point may NOT represent the whole system — especially for microbiological quality.

製藥公用系統取樣的根本挑戰在於：你在某一點量到的數值，未必能代表整個系統——尤其是微生物學品質。

Learning Objectives | 學習目標

After studying this chapter, you will be able to:
  • Explain why proper sampling is critical to pharmaceutical utility quality assurance
  • Define a "representative sample" and identify sources of sampling error
  • Distinguish the five purposes of sampling programs
  • Apply the concept of uniform vs. non-uniform quality attribute distribution
  • Differentiate chemical (homogeneous) from biological (heterogeneous) quality attributes
  • Define in-line, on-line, at-line, and off-line monitoring
  • Explain Alert Level (2σ) and Action Level (3σ) thresholds
完成本章學習後，你將能夠：
  • 說明為什麼適當的取樣對製藥公用系統品質保證至關重要
  • 定義「代表性樣品」並識別取樣誤差的來源
  • 區別取樣計畫的五個目的
  • 應用均勻與非均勻品質屬性分佈的概念
  • 區分化學（均質）與生物（異質）品質屬性
  • 定義在線、線上、近線與離線監測
  • 解釋警示限（2σ）與行動限（3σ）閾值
1.1

Background | 背景

Why effective sampling matters — and what goes wrong when it fails

Original Text (English)

Effective sampling is of paramount importance to the success of any pharmaceutical critical utility system. Unfortunately, there is very little regulatory guidance with regards to sampling. Extracting a representative sample from a utility system is an involved and complicated process and error may be introduced due to:

  • Environmental conditions
  • Sample valve design
  • Sample point location
  • Technique
  • Container type
  • Sample handling
  • Sample storage and transport
  • Other factors

The impact of these factors is widespread and occurs throughout industry. Errors due to sampling are so common that the 1993 US FDA "Guide to the Inspection of High Purity Water Systems" specifically addresses sampling errors in recommendations to their field inspectors by stating that:

"It is expected that [Water For Injection systems] be essentially sterile. Since sampling frequently is performed in non-sterile areas and is not truly aseptic, occasional low level [bacteria] counts due to sampling errors may occur." — US FDA, Guide to the Inspection of High Purity Water Systems, 1993

Improper sampling may be responsible for generating Out Of Specification (OOS) data and prompting investigations when a system is actually producing and delivering acceptable quality. Conversely, improper sampling may also create a more dangerous scenario where the quality is actually OOS but the data incorrectly indicates that the quality is acceptable.

In either case, there could be negative impact on company image, cost, productivity, ethics, and regulatory liability, resulting from improper sampling. Identifying the elements of proper sampling and eliminating the underlying reasons for these negative consequences formed the primary driving force behind this ISPE Good Practice Guide.

中文解析與實務導讀

核心主題：為什麼取樣如此重要？

製藥廠的公用系統（注射用水、純化水、蒸汽、壓縮空氣）是產品品質的基石。問題在於：你永遠無法對整個系統做全面測試——你只能取一小杯水來代表整個管路系統。

這個「代表性」的假設，就是所有問題的起點。

重要監管背景：1993 FDA 指南

FDA 在 1993 年就認知到取樣誤差的普遍性，並告訴其現場稽查員：偶爾出現低菌數，可能是取樣誤差，而非系統真正受汙染。

這是一個罕見的例子：監管機構承認「量測行為本身」就會引入誤差。這個認知在 30 年後的今天仍然是業界挑戰。

雙向風險——兩種錯誤同樣危險

  • 偽陽性 OOS（False Positive）：系統本身沒問題，但取樣誤差讓數據顯示超標 → 觸發不必要的 OOS 調查、停產、人力浪費
  • 偽陰性 OOS（False Negative）：系統真的有問題，但取樣沒取到汙染點 → 數據顯示合格 → 問題被掩蓋，藥品安全風險上升

後者在道德與法規責任上的風險遠高於前者。

CDMO 實務應用

在 CDMO 環境中，取樣誤差的後果更為複雜：你的客戶（品牌藥廠）會審查你的 OOS 調查報告，任何取樣相關的 OOS 都會影響合約關係與稽查評分。建立「取樣誤差」的完整根因分析 SOP，是品質系統成熟度的重要指標。

思考練習 Practice Questions

  1. 你的工廠目前有哪些取樣誤差的來源？請從八個錯誤來源中，挑出最可能在你的 WFI 取樣點發生的三個。
  2. 如果你是 QC 微生物人員，取到一個異常高菌數的 WFI 樣品，你會如何區分「真實汙染」與「取樣誤差」？
  3. FDA 1993 年的說法對你有什麼啟示？這種監管立場對你的 OOS 調查程序有何影響？
1.1.1

What is a Sample? | 何謂樣品？

Defining the intent and inherent limitation of sampling

Original Text (English)

Simply stated, the intent of sampling is to take a small but representative portion of a much larger stream, where the sample collected accurately represents the content of the larger stream.

The sample collected should not be altered or changed in any way because the sampling process, but this is an almost impossibly difficult proposition as all sampled utilities come into contact with air, containers, etc. during the sampling process.

中文解析與實務導讀

核心定義：代表性樣品 Representative Sample

樣品的本質：從龐大系統中取出一小部分，而這一小部分必須忠實地反映整個系統的特性。

這聽起來簡單，但原文立刻指出：這幾乎是不可能做到的完美目標。因為任何取樣動作都會讓樣品接觸到外界（空氣、容器、接頭），從而改變樣品本身的狀態。

比喻：廚師試菜

想像主廚要從一大鍋湯中嚐一口來判斷整鍋湯的鹹度。如果：

  • 湯的成分是均勻溶解的（鹽、糖）→ 任何一口都能代表整鍋
  • 湯裡有沉到底的食材（肉塊）→ 只舀表面永遠不知道底部有什麼

製藥取樣也是一樣：化學成分如鹽分，生物成分如肉塊。這個比喻將在 1.1.6 節完整展開。

重要認知：取樣動作本身就是干擾

原文明確承認：「所有被取樣的公用系統，在取樣過程中都會接觸到空氣、容器等」。這意味著：

  • 微生物取樣 → 空氣中的細菌可能進入
  • TOC 取樣 → 容器本身可能釋出有機物
  • 電導度取樣 → 容器材質、沖洗不足都會影響結果

這正是本指南存在的理由：告訴你如何將這些干擾最小化。

思考練習 Practice Questions

  1. 你工廠的 WFI 取樣容器（採樣瓶）是否有標準化規範？材質、體積、預處理方式是否有 SOP？
  2. 當你的微生物檢驗員在非無菌環境中開蓋取樣，這個動作會引入什麼樣的風險？如何量化這個風險？
  3. 「代表性樣品」在統計學上的要求是什麼？單一取樣點能代表整個分配迴路嗎？
1.1.2

Why Do We Sample? | 為何取樣？

The five purposes of pharmaceutical utility sampling programs

Original Text (English)

It is most desirable to monitor quality parameters using in-line, on-line, or at-line monitors, which minimize and, in some cases, eliminate, sample handling issues completely. However, when the quality attribute of concern cannot be analyzed with an instrument or where an instrument is not present, a sample has to be removed from a stream and evaluated off-line. In most cases, these attributes are microbiological or endotoxin in nature.

Sampling generally occurs for one or more of the following reasons:

  • Regulatory requirements — compendial requirements for CQAs
  • Quality control purposes — ensure utility meets established quality parameters; samples collected exactly as the utility is used in manufacturing
  • Process control purposes — confirm a particular process is operating under a state of control; frequency differs from QC sampling
  • Technical, investigational or diagnostic purposes — triggered by Alert Level excursions; as-needed basis
  • Test method validation purposes — periodic duplicate sampling to document consistency
Note: There is no purpose classified as "sampling for informational purposes only." Every sample point should have a specific purpose. The authors recommend abandoning this designation as being too vague and non-specific.

When developing a sampling program, a risk-based approach should be utilized to establish or adjust sampling frequencies based on data collected over time. Alert (2σ) and Action (3σ) Levels are established based on actual operating conditions.

中文解析與實務導讀

監測層級：四種監測方式

微生物與內毒素測試因技術限制，目前幾乎只能 off-line。這就是為什麼取樣技術對這些屬性特別重要。

五大取樣目的——各有不同的頻率與位置邏輯

  • 法規符合性取樣：頻率由藥典或主管機關規定；屬於合規基本要求，不可省略
  • 品質管制取樣：模擬製造使用方式取樣；必須測試該級別所有規定品質屬性
  • 製程管制取樣：確認純化步驟效能；只需測試該步驟針對的汙染物，不必測所有屬性
  • 調查診斷取樣：當警示限觸發時才啟動；頻率不固定，依需求而定
  • 方法驗證取樣：定期重複取樣，驗證方法本身的一致性

比喻：健康檢查 vs. 急診

法規符合性取樣 = 每年例行健康檢查（固定頻率、固定項目）

品質管制取樣 = 出院前的最終健康確認（確保達到標準才放行）

製程管制取樣 = 手術中的生命徵象監測（只監測手術相關指標）

調查診斷取樣 = 急診（有症狀才去，針對症狀做檢查）

方法驗證取樣 = 校正量血壓計（確認測量工具本身準確）

廢棄「僅供參考」取樣的意義

ISPE 明確建議廢除「for informational purposes only」這個分類。原因是：

  • 沒有目的的數據，就無法定義合格標準
  • 模糊的分類容易被監管機關質疑
  • 每個取樣點都應有明確的決策邏輯

這對 CDMO 尤其重要——客戶的稽查員會問：「這個取樣點的目的是什麼？超標怎麼辦？」

警示限與行動限：2σ 與 3σ

Alert Level（警示限）= 2σ：系統可能偏離正常範圍的警告信號，不一定需要立即採取糾正措施，但需要監控與記錄。

Action Level（行動限）= 3σ：系統已偏離正常範圍，必須採取糾正措施使系統回到受控狀態。

這些限值是根據實際操作數據建立的，不是憑空設定。有效的取樣計畫能讓你累積足夠的歷史數據，讓限值有統計意義。

思考練習 Practice Questions

  1. 你工廠的 WFI 取樣計畫中，每個取樣點的「目的」是否有明確文件記載？這五個目的各佔多少比例？
  2. 品質管制取樣要求「完全複製製造使用方式」，這在實際操作中有哪些挑戰？你的現有 SOP 是否滿足這個要求？
  3. 你的 WFI 系統目前的 Alert 和 Action Level 是如何建立的？是基於統計數據還是直接引用藥典限值？
1.1.3

Who is Responsible? | 責任歸屬

Quality control leads, but multiple stakeholders are involved

Original Text (English)

Ultimately, the quality control function is responsible for sampling, but other stakeholders may become involved with sampling including:

  • Quality assurance
  • Utilities / Facilities
  • Manufacturing / Production
  • Regulatory affairs
中文解析與實務導讀

跨功能責任矩陣

原文強調最終責任在 QC，但取樣計畫的設計與執行涉及多個部門。在 CDMO 環境中，這尤其複雜，因為你同時要面對自己的 QA 系統和客戶的品質期望。

工程師的角色：常被忽略但極關鍵

本指南特別提到 utilities 和 facilities 工程師。這是因為：取樣閥的設計、位置、材質、安裝方式，是決定樣品是否具代表性的先決條件。工程師在系統設計階段就必須考慮取樣需求，而不是在系統建成後再想辦法。

這也是為什麼 ISPE 指南的讀者群包含設計工程師——取樣品質從設計開始。

思考練習 Practice Questions

  1. 在你的組織中，當 WFI 系統發生取樣相關的 OOS 時，各部門的角色和責任是否有明確的 RACI 矩陣？
  2. 你的工廠設施工程師是否參與了取樣計畫的設計？他們了解取樣閥設計對微生物取樣結果的影響嗎？
  3. 當 QC、QA 和生產對取樣時程有衝突時，誰有最終決定權？這個決策程序是否文件化？
1.1.4

How Often Do We Need to Sample? | 取樣頻率

Risk-based frequency determination for different utility grades

Original Text (English)

Sampling frequency depends on the system and the grade of the critical utility.

For Water For Injection (WFI): it is an expectation that water samples will be taken from each Point Of Use (POU) and sample location in the distribution system at least once per week during validation. Industry has continued to utilize this same sampling frequency beyond the completion of the Performance Qualification, although it is not mandated.

By contrast, purified water has no such preconceived sampling requirements, so the end user is not mandated to follow any specific schedule during or following validation.

Pharmaceutical steam, compressed air, and process gases have different frequencies during validation and ongoing operation.

When no sampling frequency is specified, a risk-based approach may be utilized in conjunction with the purpose of sampling to establish initial sampling frequencies. As data is generated and an operating baseline is established, the collected data should be reviewed to determine if the operating limits, Alert and Action Levels, and/or the sampling frequency may be adjusted (increased or decreased) based on data generated on system operation.

中文解析與實務導讀

不同公用系統的取樣頻率比較

風險導向頻率調整：數據說話

原文提到一個重要概念：取樣頻率不是固定不變的，而是應該隨著數據積累而動態調整。

  • 初始階段：頻率較高，建立操作基準線
  • 穩定階段：如果數據顯示系統受控，可以降低頻率
  • 風險上升時：如季節變化、消毒後、系統維修後，應增加頻率

這種動態調整需要有完整的趨勢分析系統作為支撐。

CDMO 實務：PQ 後的頻率決策

WFI 每週取樣是「業界期望」不是「法規強制」。很多 CDMO 在 PQ 完成後仍保持每週頻率，這是因為：

  • 客戶合約通常要求符合業界最佳實務
  • 稽查員默認這個頻率，降低頻率需要有強有力的風險評估文件支持
  • WFI 是最高風險的公用系統，保守策略是合理的

思考練習 Practice Questions

  1. 你的工廠 WFI 取樣計畫是否有明確的「頻率調整觸發條件」？什麼情況下你會增加/減少頻率？
  2. PQ 結束後，你是否曾經合理地降低了 WFI 取樣頻率？這個決定有什麼風險評估文件支撐？
  3. 壓縮空氣和製程氣體的取樣頻率在你的工廠是如何決定的？是否有獨立的風險評估？
1.1.5

Where Do We Need to Sample? | 取樣位置

Location selection driven by purpose and engineering judgment

Original Text (English)

Sampling locations are determined by the purpose of sampling and the information expected from the sampling location. Careful consideration and sound engineering judgment should be utilized to distinguish between sampling locations for:

  • Regulatory Compliance
  • Quality Control
  • Process Control
  • Investigational and Diagnostic purposes
中文解析與實務導讀

「目的決定位置」的邏輯

取樣位置不是隨機選定的，而是由取樣目的反推出來的。每個取樣閥安裝的理由，都應該對應一個明確的取樣目的。

  • 法規符合性位置：通常是 Point of Use (POU)，即製造使用點
  • 製程管制位置：通常在純化步驟的中間點（如 RO 膜出口、UV 處理後）
  • 調查位置：根據問題假設決定，事先規劃但按需啟用

工程判斷的重要性

原文強調「sound engineering judgment」。這不是一句空話——工程師必須理解流體力學、死角（dead leg）的形成、管路設計對微生物累積的影響，才能正確判斷取樣位置的代表性。

例如：一個位於系統最低點、水流速度最慢的取樣閥，可能比位於高流速主管路上的取樣閥更容易出現微生物超標——但這不代表系統有問題，只是位置選擇的問題。

思考練習 Practice Questions

  1. 你工廠的 WFI 分配迴路中，是否有任何「死角」？這些位置是否有取樣點？
  2. 你的取樣計畫中，每個取樣點的目的是否有明確文件記錄？是否能對應到上述四種目的之一？
  3. 如果明天你的 WFI 系統出現微生物超標，你的 SOP 中有哪些「調查診斷」取樣位置可以立即啟用？
1.1.6

Are All Quality Attributes Uniformly Distributed? | 品質屬性是否均勻分佈？

The most critical paradigm shift in pharmaceutical utility sampling

Paradigm Shift Alert | 觀念革新

The answer is a resounding NO — and this is one of the most important paradigm shifts that the reader should understand.

答案是斷然的「否」——這是讀者在評估取樣計畫時必須理解的最重要觀念轉變之一。

Original Text (English)

The answer is a resounding no, and this is one of the most important paradigm shifts that the reader should understand when defining and evaluating a sampling program.

In pharmaceutical water systems:

  • If a quality attribute is a chemical constituent (e.g., nitrates, conductivity, dissolved metals, TOC) then the constituent is considered uniformly or homogeneously distributed (Second Law of Thermodynamics).
  • However, if the quality attribute is biological in nature (e.g., bacteria, endotoxin), then the quality attribute will not be uniformly distributed. Non-uniform or heterogeneously distributed attributes are much more challenging to sample accurately as these attributes may vary from point to point in a system.

A significant portion of this Guide is devoted to providing guidance on the most effective methods for accurate sample collection involving these heterogeneously distributed quality attributes.

In pharmaceutical steam systems, compressed air, and process gas systems, attributes may or may not be uniformly distributed and sampling programs must take this into account.

中文解析與實務導讀

兩類品質屬性的本質差異

熱力學第二定律——為什麼化學成分是均勻的？

化學成分溶解在水中後，分子自然趨向均勻分佈（熵增大）。電導度代表離子濃度，硝酸鹽代表分子濃度——這些分子在液態水中以布朗運動持續運動，最終達到熱力學平衡。

換句話說：如果你的 WFI 管路中電導度超標，你在任何一個取樣點都會量到超標，因為電導度是均勻分佈的。

為什麼細菌是非均勻分佈的？

細菌不是化學分子——它們是活的生物體，具有以下行為：

  • 表面附著（adhesion）：細菌會主動或被動地附著在管路內壁、死角、閥門密封面等表面。附著的細菌不在液相中流動。
  • 生物膜形成（biofilm）：附著的細菌分泌多醣基質，形成生物膜。生物膜中的細菌數量可以是流體中懸浮菌數的 1000 倍以上。
  • 群落分佈（colony formation）：細菌以群落生長，不是均勻散佈——某個死角可能有大量細菌，而幾公分外的管路可能完全無菌。
  • 剝落（detachment）：生物膜中的細菌在流速變化、溫度衝擊（如消毒）時會大量剝落，進入液相，造成某個時間點的菌數爆衝。
Key Concept: Heterogeneous Distribution Explained

Analogy: Salt vs. Fish in the Ocean

Imagine the ocean:

  • Salt (NaCl): Uniformly dissolved throughout — a sample from any depth or location gives you the same salinity reading. Salt behaves like a chemical attribute.
  • Fish: Clustered in schools, near reefs, at specific depths — you could cast a net 10 times and catch nothing, then cast it in the same area a minute later and pull up hundreds. Fish behave like biological attributes.

If you're measuring the "fish quality" of the ocean, one sample from one spot at one time tells you almost nothing about the whole. The same applies to bacteria in a pharmaceutical water system.

Implications for Endotoxin

Endotoxin (lipopolysaccharide, LPS) is the cell wall fragment of gram-negative bacteria. Its distribution in a water system follows the same heterogeneous pattern as bacteria — because endotoxin is released when bacteria die or shed their membranes, it tends to concentrate where bacteria concentrate.

However, endotoxin is more complex: once released into the water, it can aggregate and disaggregate depending on temperature, pH, and ionic strength. This further complicates representative sampling.

比喻解析與 CDMO 意涵

海洋比喻的深層含義

鹽 = 化學屬性：不管在大西洋哪裡取樣，鹽度大致相同。你只需要取一個樣品就能了解整個系統的鹽度水平。

魚 = 生物屬性：魚群聚集在礁石旁、特定水深、特定季節。你在同一片海域取樣十次，可能九次空手而回，一次大豐收。這不代表海裡「沒有魚」或「魚的品質有問題」——只是你取樣的時間和地點沒有捕捉到魚群的位置。

關鍵結論：對生物屬性而言，你在哪裡取樣、什麼時候取樣，和你量到什麼，密不可分。一個負結果不等於整個系統沒有問題。

對 CDMO 無菌充填廠的深遠影響

  • WFI 迴路中的「熱點」：即使你的多個 POU 取樣都合格，某個低流速的支管或死角仍可能有生物膜存在。這是真實系統中的「魚」——你沒有捕到，不代表不存在。
  • OOS 調查的複雜性：一個 WFI POU 點的微生物超標，原因可能完全不在那個點——生物膜從上游某個死角剝落，隨水流到了那個取樣點。取樣位置不等於問題來源。
  • 消毒後取樣策略：消毒（sanitization）後，死亡細菌的細胞壁碎片（即內毒素）會大量釋放入水中。這段時間的 WFI 可能微生物合格但內毒素超標——因為兩者的分佈模式不同。
  • 稽查準備：FDA 和 EMA 的稽查員越來越精通取樣非均勻性的概念。他們可能質疑你的取樣位置是否真正能代表系統的微生物風險。

實務行動：如何應對非均勻分佈

  • 確保取樣點覆蓋系統最高風險位置（死角、低流速區、溫度最低點）
  • 不要只取 POU 樣品——設計兼顧製程管制位置的取樣計畫
  • 定期分析趨勢：某個取樣點持續偏高，可能是上游生物膜的徵兆
  • 消毒前後的取樣策略要分開設計

思考練習 Practice Questions

  1. 你的 WFI 分配系統中，哪些位置最可能形成生物膜？這些位置是否在你的定期取樣計畫中？
  2. 如果你的一個 WFI 取樣點微生物數值突然升高，但所有其他點都正常，你的第一反應是什麼？這是「取樣誤差」還是「局部生物膜剝落」？如何區分？
  3. 你的工廠在 WFI 系統消毒後，有特別設計的「消毒後取樣計畫」嗎？這個計畫是否考慮到內毒素的非均勻分佈特性？
  4. 為什麼電導度超標和微生物超標需要完全不同的根因分析策略？請用本節的概念來解釋。
1.2

Overview | 概覽

Who this guide affects and what industries it covers

Original Text (English)

This Guide affects users of water, steam, compressed air, or process gases and impacts facilities, production, and quality control personnel within a facility.

This Guide applies to manufacturers of:

  • Pharmaceuticals
  • Medical devices
  • Biologics
  • Cosmetics and related products

As well as equipment manufacturers, vendors, and other industries outside of the pharmaceutical arena.

中文解析與實務導讀

適用範圍的廣度

本指南不只是給製藥廠用的。醫療器材、生物製劑、化妝品製造商，甚至設備供應商，都在適用範圍內。這反映了一個現實：公用系統的取樣挑戰是跨產業的共同問題。

CDMO 特殊情境：多客戶、多產品

CDMO 同時為製藥、生物製劑、醫療器材客戶提供服務時，可能面對不同的取樣標準和期望。本指南的跨產業適用性，意味著你可以用同一套框架應對不同客戶的審計要求。

關鍵是建立一套足夠嚴格的基準取樣系統，能夠滿足最嚴格的客戶要求，並在必要時向較寬鬆的客戶解釋你的方法。

思考練習 Practice Questions

  1. 你的 CDMO 目前的公用系統取樣計畫，是否已考慮到不同客戶產品類型的差異化需求？
  2. 設備供應商也在本指南的適用範圍內——這意味著你在採購新取樣閥或取樣系統時，應該要求供應商說明什麼？
  3. 化妝品製造商的公用系統要求與製藥廠有何不同？這種差異如何影響取樣設計？
1.3

Scope and Purpose | 範圍與目的

What this guide covers — and where it stops

Original Text (English)

This Guide has been assembled to provide assistance to designer engineers, process engineers, facilities engineers, quality assurance staff, quality control staff, production staff, and any other group, team, or individual that may be impacted by the results of a sampling program.

This Guide covers the critical utilities of:

  • Pharmaceutical water
  • Pharmaceutical steam
  • Pharmaceutical process gases

This Guide covers all aspects of sampling from:

  • Valve design
  • Number, location, and placement of sample valves
  • Sampling technique
  • Frequency
  • Sample storage including delivery to the testing laboratory

Scope boundary: The scope of this Guide stops when the sample is delivered to the laboratory for analysis. This Guide does not include the actual testing performed after the sample is turned over to the laboratory, nor does it cover data interpretation or analysis.

This Guide does not cover:

  • HVAC systems for cleanrooms
  • Environmental monitoring
  • Active Pharmaceutical Ingredients (APIs)
  • Finished products
中文解析與實務導讀

範圍邊界的重要性

本指南有一個非常清晰的邊界：樣品送到實驗室時，本指南的責任就結束。之後的分析方法、數據解讀、統計分析，由其他指南（如 USP 方法指南）涵蓋。

這個邊界的設定非常實際：取樣過程和分析過程是兩個獨立的品質關鍵步驟，混在一起討論反而會讓責任模糊。

工程師是核心讀者——為什麼？

本指南明確將「設計工程師」列為第一讀者群。這是因為取樣品質的基礎在於設計，而不是操作。

  • 取樣閥的設計決定了是否會有死水（stagnant water）累積
  • 取樣點的位置決定了樣品是否具有代表性
  • 管路材質和表面粗糙度影響生物膜形成

一個設計不良的取樣系統，無論操作多麼規範，都無法獲得真正有意義的樣品。

不在範圍內的項目——同樣需要了解

本指南不涵蓋：

  • 潔淨室 HVAC 環境監測 → 另見 ISO 14644、PIC/S Annex 1
  • API 和成品取樣 → 另見 ICH Q7、各藥典

了解這些邊界，幫助你在稽查時明確知道：「這個問題屬於哪一個 SOP 的管轄範圍」，避免文件之間的灰色地帶。

思考練習 Practice Questions

  1. 你的工廠目前的取樣 SOP 是否清楚界定了「取樣」和「分析」的責任邊界？樣品移交實驗室的程序是否有文件化？
  2. 你的設計工程師在參與新設備或新管路設計時，是否有考慮取樣點的設計規範？取樣閥的選型是否有標準？
  3. HVAC 環境監測和公用系統取樣是否有整合的監控策略？還是各自獨立管理？
1.4

Benefits | 效益

The business case for investing in proper sampling practices

Original Text (English)

This Guide aims to:

  • Provide industry with standards and best practices for sampling in a comprehensive single reference.
  • Help to minimize sampling errors and their contribution to Out of Specification (OOS) results, which can cause costly work and production stoppages, investigations, and disruptions in manufacturing, Quality Control (QC)/Quality Assurance (QA), and engineering organizations.

This Guide is expected to be of benefit to laboratory, QC/QA, engineering, facilities, and operations personnel.

中文解析與實務導讀

效益的商業邏輯

改善取樣做法的效益，可以從三個維度量化：

  • 成本節省：減少偽陽性 OOS → 減少不必要的調查費用、停產損失
  • 品質提升：減少偽陰性 OOS → 減少真實品質問題被掩蓋的風險
  • 法規合規：有完善取樣系統的工廠在 FDA/EMA 稽查中更容易通過

CDMO 視角：OOS 的成本

一次 WFI 微生物 OOS 調查的直接成本，在中型 CDMO 中通常包括：

  • QA/QC 人員調查時間（通常 20-40 小時）
  • 額外取樣和測試費用
  • 生產延遲（如果因此停產）
  • 客戶溝通和文件準備

如果最終確認是「取樣誤差」，這些成本全部是可以避免的。投資在取樣訓練和設備上，ROI 非常明確。

思考練習 Practice Questions

  1. 過去一年，你的工廠有多少 OOS 最終被歸因於「取樣誤差」？這些調查總共花費了多少人時？
  2. 如果能將取樣相關的 OOS 減少 50%，你估計每年能為工廠節省多少成本？
  3. 你的工廠是否定期對取樣人員進行資格確認（qualification）？這個訓練計畫是否有文件化的能力評估？
1.5

Objectives | 目標

What this guide is designed to accomplish

Original Text (English)

This Guide aims to establish good practices for sampling to minimize sample contamination from:

  • Human contact
  • Error
  • Atmospheric or environmental conditions

Which could alter laboratory results and provide inaccurate data.

中文解析與實務導讀

污染源的三個類別

  • 人員接觸（Human contact）：手套的微粒、呼吸中的微生物、觸碰瓶口等——人是最大的取樣汙染源之一
  • 操作誤差（Error）：沖洗時間不足、沖洗液未完全排淨、採樣順序錯誤
  • 環境條件（Atmospheric/environmental）：在非無菌環境中開蓋取樣、空調出風口正對取樣點、溫濕度影響樣品穩定性

人員是最難控制的變量

機器的行為是可預測的，但人員的行為取決於訓練、態度、當天的工作狀態。這就是為什麼：

  • 取樣 SOP 必須有詳細的步驟圖解，不能只有文字
  • 取樣人員必須定期接受再訓練和能力評估
  • 微生物取樣應由受過無菌技術訓練的人員執行

思考練習 Practice Questions

  1. 你的微生物取樣 SOP 中，對「沖洗時間」有具體的秒數或體積規定嗎？還是只說「充分沖洗」？
  2. 你的取樣人員是否接受過無菌取樣技術的評估？評估頻率是多少？
  3. 你的工廠是否有記錄「取樣人員 ID」在每個微生物樣品的記錄中？這個數據是否被用於趨勢分析？
1.6

Key Concepts / Terms | 核心術語

Foundational definitions used throughout the ISPE Sampling Guide

Original Definitions (English)

Alert Level 警示限

A level or range that, when exceeded, indicates that a process may have drifted from its normal operating range. May be established at two standard deviations (2σ) from the mean. Constitutes a warning and does not necessarily require a corrective action.

Action Level 行動限

A level established that, when exceeded, indicates that a process from its normal operating range. Typically established at three standard deviations (3σ) from the mean. Corrective actions should be taken to bring the process back into its normal operating range.

Contaminant / Impurity 汙染物/雜質

Contaminant: Any foreign component present in another substance; used synonymously with impurity in this Guide.

Impurity: A foreign agent that is introduced as part of a process; used synonymously with contaminant in this Guide.

Note: Additional key terms (In-line, On-line, At-line, Off-line monitoring; Representative Sample; Measurement Uncertainty) are introduced and defined in later chapters of this Guide, where they are applied in context.

術語深度解析

Alert Level vs. Action Level — 統計基礎

這兩個術語在製藥公用系統中極為常用，但必須理解其統計基礎：

  • 正態分佈假設：這些限值假設數據符合正態分佈。但微生物數據通常不是正態分佈——它往往是右偏斜的（大多數時候菌數很低，偶爾很高）。因此許多工廠對微生物數據取對數後再建立控制限。
  • 2σ（約 95.4% 信心水準）：警示限意味著在正常系統中，大約每 22 個樣品中可能有 1 個超過此限值，純粹是統計機率，不代表系統真的有問題。
  • 3σ（約 99.7% 信心水準）：行動限被超過的概率在正常系統中約為 0.3%——如果頻繁超過，系統很可能真的偏移了正常狀態。

比喻：體溫監測

把你的 WFI 系統想像成一個病人的體溫：

  • 正常範圍：36.1 – 37.2°C（對應正常操作範圍）
  • Alert Level：37.5°C（微燒，需要觀察，不需立即打針）
  • Action Level：38.5°C（發燒，需要立即採取措施）

偶爾量到 37.5°C 不需要恐慌，但如果持續出現，就要開始調查是否有潛在感染。這就是趨勢分析的意義。

監測方式術語整理（後續章節預告）

微生物和內毒素測試因技術限制，目前幾乎只能 off-line，這使得取樣程序的嚴謹性對結果的可靠性至關重要。

「代表性樣品」與「測量不確定度」的關係

每一個測量結果都有不確定度（uncertainty）。對公用系統取樣而言，不確定度來自：

  • 取樣過程的隨機誤差（人員操作差異）
  • 系統的時間變異（菌數隨時間波動）
  • 空間異質性（不同位置的真實差異）
  • 分析方法本身的誤差（培養基、培養條件）

理解測量不確定度，才能正確解讀一個「接近但未超過行動限」的結果——它代表的是一個範圍，而不是一個精確的數字。

思考練習 Practice Questions

  1. 你的工廠 WFI 系統的 Alert 和 Action Level 是基於多少個數據點建立的？這個數據量足以支撐統計意義嗎？
  2. 你的微生物數據是正態分佈嗎？如果不是，你現在使用的控制圖方法是否適用？
  3. 在實際操作中，當一個結果超過 Alert Level 但未超過 Action Level 時，你的 SOP 要求做什麼？這個回應是否有文件記錄？
  4. 你能說明 in-line TOC 分析儀和 off-line 微生物取樣在「不確定度」方面有什麼根本性的差異嗎？

Chapter 1 Summary | 第一章總結

Effective pharmaceutical utility sampling requires understanding that chemical quality attributes are uniformly distributed, while biological attributes (bacteria, endotoxin) are heterogeneous — and that sampling errors, if uncontrolled, can generate both false OOS results and dangerous false-compliant results.

有效的製藥公用系統取樣，需要理解：化學品質屬性均勻分佈，而生物屬性（細菌、內毒素）是非均勻分佈的——若不加控制的取樣誤差，可能同時產生偽陽性 OOS 結果，以及更危險的偽合格結果。

Learning Objectives | 學習目標

After studying this section you will be able to:
  • Explain why water is the most critical utility in pharmaceutical manufacturing
  • Distinguish between PW, HPW, and WFI — specifications, uses, and regulatory basis across USP, EP, and JP
  • Differentiate homogeneous vs. heterogeneous impurity distribution and its impact on sampling strategy
  • Describe the five categories of sampling purpose and match each to appropriate sampling frequency and location
  • Define Alert and Action Levels statistically (2σ / 3σ) and describe the escalation response protocol
  • Apply a risk-based approach to selecting sampling locations in a distribution loop
  • Identify microbial hot-spot locations within a water system (deadlegs, valve seats, hoses)
  • Explain the difference between process-control and quality-control sampling at POUs
學完本節後，你將能夠：
  • 說明水為何是製藥生產中最關鍵的公用物料
  • 區別 PW、HPW、WFI 的規格、用途與各藥典（USP、EP、JP）的法規依據
  • 分辨均質雜質與非均質雜質的分佈差異及其對取樣策略的影響
  • 描述取樣目的的五大類別，並將每類與適當的取樣頻率和位置對應
  • 以統計定義警戒水準（2σ）和行動水準（3σ），並描述升級回應程序
  • 在配水迴路中運用風險評估方法選擇取樣位置
  • 識別水系統中的微生物熱點（死腿、閥座、軟管）
  • 解釋 POU 的製程控制取樣與品質控制取樣之差異
2.1

Introduction | 簡介

Water as the most widely used pharmaceutical material — roles and sampling fundamentals | 水作為最廣泛使用的製藥物料

2.1 Introduction

Water is one of the most widely used materials in the pharmaceutical industry and is commonly used as a:

  • Product or Ingredient
  • Cleaning agent
  • Sterilizing media
  • Analytical agent
  • Formulation aid

When water is used for pharmaceutical purposes it needs to be tested to ensure that it meets monograph requirements or other specifications for applicable CQAs (Critical Quality Attributes). When water is extracted for sampling purposes at any point in a system, proper sampling is the key to ensuring that the collected sample accurately represents the quality of the water at that particular point in the system.

When water is sampled in the same way as it is used during manufacturing, sampling is considered the best indicator available of the quality of water going into a product.

Key Principle: Sample as You Use

The closer a sampling method mirrors actual manufacturing use, the more representative the result. This principle drives every decision in this guide — from valve selection to flushing volume to sample container choice.

Water Types in Pharmaceutical Manufacturing

All major pharmacopoeias define at minimum two compendial bulk grades:

  • Purified Water (PW) — for non-parenteral products, equipment cleaning, and general manufacturing
  • Water For Injection (WFI) — for parenteral products, ophthalmic preparations, and final equipment rinse in aseptic processing

The European Pharmacopoeia additionally defines Highly Purified Water (HPW) — meeting WFI chemical specifications but produced by a non-distillation process (e.g., double-pass RO + UF).

All pharmacopoeias (USP, EP, JP, Chinese Pharmacopoeia) require monitoring of the following CQAs:

  • Conductivity — ionic purity indicator
  • TOC (Total Organic Carbon) — organic contamination indicator
  • Endotoxin — WFI and HPW only; LAL or rFC method
  • Bioburden — not a monograph requirement, but universally tested
中文解析與 CDMO 應用 | Commentary & CDMO Context

水的五種角色

水在製藥中同時扮演五種角色：產品原料、清洗劑、滅菌介質、分析試劑、製劑輔助劑。在 CDMO 環境中，同一條水迴路可能在同一天用於多個客戶產品的配製與清洗，因此水質監控失敗的影響是跨產品的。

CQA 的定義

Critical Quality Attribute（關鍵品質屬性）是指對產品安全性、效力或品質有直接影響的物理、化學、生物或微生物特性。對於水系統而言，CQA 通常包括導電率、TOC、內毒素（WFI）和微生物含量。

比喻：水質像城市供水

想像一個城市的自來水系統：主幹管（storage tank → 配水迴路）代表整體水質，而每個水龍頭（POU）代表實際使用點。即使主幹管水質合格，末端水龍頭的橡膠墊圈或管內積水仍可能帶入微生物污染。這正是 ISPE 強調「取樣方式應模擬使用方式」的原因。

CDMO 實務：多客戶水系統的挑戰

在多品種 CDMO 廠，PW 和 WFI 迴路服務不同客戶產品線。取樣策略必須考慮：

  • 不同客戶對水規格的個別要求（可能高於藥典）
  • 共用迴路的污染風險（清洗驗證 + 水質確認）
  • 高峰生產時多個 POU 同時使用，水壓和流速變化對微生物的影響

法規重點：「以使用方式取樣」

FDA 1993 年檢查指南明確要求：水的取樣方式應盡可能複製製造時的使用方式。這意味著如果生產時會連接軟管和熱交換器，取樣時也應如此操作——否則取樣結果不具代表性，在偏差調查中將受到質疑。

Practice Questions | 練習思考

  1. A CDMO site has a single WFI loop serving both aseptic fill-finish and lyophilizer loading. What are the primary CQAs you would monitor, and why is endotoxin particularly critical for this loop? （一條 WFI 迴路同時服務無菌灌裝和凍乾機裝料，主要 CQA 為何？為何內毒素特別關鍵？）
  2. The guide states that water sampled the same way as used in manufacturing is "the best indicator of quality going into a product." Why would an upstream sample port on a POU valve NOT satisfy this requirement for microbial testing? （為何 POU 閥上游的取樣埠無法滿足微生物取樣的代表性要求？）
  3. Your PW system serves a washer (non-parenteral), a formulation tank (oral), and a buffer prep vessel (injectable). Should they all use the same sampling protocol? Justify your answer. （三個不同用途的 POU 應使用相同取樣規程嗎？說明理由。）
2.1.1

Homogeneously Distributed Impurities | 均質分佈雜質

Chemical impurities, conductivity, TOC — same concentration throughout the loop | 化學雜質在整個迴路中均勻分佈

2.1.1.1 Homogeneously Distributed Impurities

Chemical impurities, small particulates, and other soluble impurities are typically expected to be homogeneously distributed throughout a distribution system because of the solubility and nature of these impurities, and because of chemical equilibrium processes.

Since the impurity levels at any one location in a distribution system should be identical to the impurity levels at every other location within the distribution system, sampling for homogeneously distributed impurities may not be required at every POU and may be performed at a limited number of locations, provided that there is no likelihood of downstream sources of contamination.

Homogeneously distributed impurities are candidates for continuous monitoring using on-line, in-line, or at-line instruments if the impurity levels at the instrumentation locations have been validated through sampling and laboratory analysis to be predictive of the levels at all POUs.

Sampling and testing of these impurities is typically done at the return of a distribution loop, but may be done in other locations. Impurities falling into the homogeneously distributed category include:

  • Ionic impurities (detected as electrical conductivity or resistivity)
  • Organic impurities (detected as TOC)
  • Nitrates (EP requirement for PW and WFI)
  • Heavy metals (EP requirement for PW — not required if conductivity meets WFI limits)
"Localized sources of chemical impurities may be introduced to a system downstream of a particular point... such as from hoses, gaskets, or a POU heat exchanger may contaminate the water as it exits the system at one particular location."

Sub-loops, parallel loops, or other isolated portions may not be accurately represented by on-line instrumentation in the main distribution system. In these cases, additional instruments or manual POU testing may be required.

2.1.1.2 Heterogeneously Distributed Impurities

Bacteria and endotoxin are attributes that are not uniformly distributed throughout a water system. The majority of bacteria present in the system (99.9 to 99.99%) reside in biofilm — attached to system surfaces, not free-floating.

It is the small fraction (0.01 to 0.1%) of free floating or planktonic bacteria that contribute to the bacteria and endotoxin levels detected by sampling.

Biofilm development occurs more rapidly in areas of low or no flow. Examples of low-flow areas that allow bacteria to attach include:

  • Within any non-flowing side connections of any length, including dead legs
  • On the upstream/wet side of valve sealing surfaces
  • On the water-stopping sealing surfaces within the valve
  • On the downstream side of valve surfaces (which may remain wet or moist)
  • On fittings and gaskets used to connect a hose or other connector
  • Within the hose or connector to the actual location of water use
  • Within any additional external device: flow meters, pressure regulators, heat exchangers, check valves, hoses, fittings, adapters

Because of variable local flow conditions, bacteria and endotoxin populations may vary widely at different locations. Therefore, sampling is required of each POU location to confirm the presence or absence of bacteria. Sampling only the supply and return is insufficient to characterize bacterial populations throughout the system.

中文解析：均質 vs 非均質雜質的策略含義

均質雜質（Homogeneous）

關鍵結論：導電率和 TOC 在迴路中濃度一致，因此可以用迴路回流口的在線儀表替代逐一 POU 手動取樣。這是製藥水系統中重要的連續監控合理性依據。但必須先通過取樣驗證，確認儀表位置的讀數確實代表所有 POU 的濃度。

例外情況：子迴路污染

如果某個子迴路（sub-loop）或 POU 下游有可能引入化學污染（如：軟管的塑化劑析出、橡膠墊圈的有機物溶出），則主迴路的在線儀表無法偵測到這些局部污染。必須在子迴路或 POU 處增加手動取樣或獨立儀表。

非均質雜質（Heterogeneous）— 生物膜的真相

系統中 99.9–99.99% 的細菌存在於生物膜（biofilm）中，附著在管壁、閥座等表面，而非懸浮在水中。取樣只能偵測到浮游（planktonic）細菌——僅佔系統總菌量的 0.01–0.1%。

實務含義：低菌計數不代表系統清潔；若生物膜在某次衝擊（溫度變化、流速突增）後脫落，計數可能突然飆升。這是為何警戒/行動水準和趨勢分析比單次結果更重要。

CDMO 高風險場景：死腿與慢流區

在設計複雜的多產品廠房中，管道佈局往往形成「臨時死腿」——例如長期不使用的 POU 支管、停用的設備連接管。ISPE 明確指出這些是生物膜熱點。CDMO 操作員必須：

  • 定期沖洗或封閉停用的 POU（lock out / tag out）
  • 在恢復使用前執行微生物取樣確認
  • 將死腿長度控制在 3D 以內（管徑的 3 倍，工業慣例）

比喻：生物膜像淋浴蓮蓬頭的水垢

長期不使用的蓮蓬頭內部會積累生物膜（即俗稱的「水垢微生物」）。當你打開水龍頭的瞬間，大量細菌被沖出——這就是「過夜停滯（overnight stagnation）」對 WFI 系統的危害。製藥水系統的解決方案：保持循環流速、定期熱水消毒或週期性蒸汽滅菌。

Practice Questions | 練習思考

  1. Your WFI loop has 12 POUs. For conductivity monitoring, how many locations do you actually need to sample manually, assuming a validated in-line instrument is installed at the loop return? Justify your answer citing the principle of homogeneous distribution. （假設迴路回流口安裝了已驗證的在線導電率儀，手動取樣幾個位置就足夠？）
  2. A QC analyst finds low bioburden (<1 cfu/100 mL) in a WFI loop for 6 consecutive months. Is it safe to conclude the system has no biofilm risk? Why or why not? （6個月連續低菌計數是否代表系統沒有生物膜風險？）
  3. Describe two engineering controls you would specify during detailed design to minimize deadleg formation in a WFI distribution loop serving 8 manufacturing suites. （描述兩種在詳細設計階段減少死腿形成的工程管控措施。）
2.1.2

Purpose of Sampling | 取樣目的

Five categories: regulatory, consensus standards, process control, quality control, investigative | 五類取樣目的

2.1.2 Purpose of Sampling

The purpose of sampling should be identified and documented for each potential sample location within a system as early as possible during the design process. This process should justify and document the requirement for sampling and identify the reason for sampling at a particular location.

The purpose of any potential sampling location should fall into one or more of the following categories:

  1. Regulatory requirements
  2. Consensus standards
  3. Process control purposes
  4. Quality control purposes
  5. Technical, investigational, or diagnostic purposes

The justification for a potential sampling location should also consider:

  • The impurities of interest at the potential location
  • The type of valve and other accessories best suited for the location
  • Whether sampling should be performed at an established frequency or on an event-based frequency (i.e., reaching an alert or action level)
  • Accessibility to staff and safety considerations
  • Any special considerations for sample handling after collection

2.1.2.1 Regulatory Requirements

All pharmacopoeias define two bulk grades of water for pharmaceutical purposes: Purified Water (PW) and Water For Injection (WFI). Highly Purified Water (HPW) is an additional grade defined by the European Pharmacopoeia.

The general consensus across pharmacopoeias is that the following impurities should be monitored:

  • Conductivity
  • TOC
  • Endotoxin (for WFI only)

Some pharmacopoeias also require testing for heavy metals and nitrates. While bacteria testing is not a monograph requirement, all pharmaceutical companies sample and test for bacteria.

The pharmaceutical industry references the 1993 US FDA "Guide to the Inspection of High Purity Water Systems" which stipulates the following maximum bacteria action limits:

  • PW: ≤ 100 cfu/mL
  • WFI: ≤ 10 cfu/100 mL

The pharmaceutical industry has universally adopted these limits. Thus, water systems are routinely sampled and tested for: Conductivity, TOC, Endotoxin (WFI only), and Bacteria.

2.1.2.2 Consensus Standards

Consensus standards such as ISO, ASTM, AAMI, and CLSI have application-specific standards for water purity. These may apply where the use of water within the facility is consistent with those standards. Water quality specifications from these standards may be found in Appendix 1 of the guide.

2.1.2.3 Process Control Purposes

Monitoring a water purification system for process control involves monitoring the performance and success of the various treatment processes for specific attributes of concern and includes following the quantitative trends of those attributes.

Process control indicating trigger values, such as Alert Levels and Action Levels, are typically used to assist in identifying when the process is deviating from its normal operating capabilities.

Alert Levels

Alert Levels should be set at levels near the top edge of normal data trends — typically at two standard deviations (2σ) from normal operating levels, based on analysis of historic performance data.

An occasional Alert Level excursion barely above the limit could be a normal expectation within the upper reaches of normal operating trends. However, frequent excursions should be considered out of trend. Responses include notification of quality, manufacturing, and maintenance personnel, along with closer attention to routine data.

Action Levels

Action Levels are typically set at three standard deviations (3σ) from normal operating levels. They should be:

  • Above normal data trends and indicative of routine process controls beginning to fail
  • Far enough from the specification so that remedial action can restore control before a specification excursion occurs

Resampling and retesting should be one of the first corrective actions. Where high values are confirmed, appropriate remediation activities should be instituted and the cause(s) determined to preclude recurrence.

中文解析：取樣目的的五大類別

為什麼要在設計初期確認取樣目的？

ISPE 強調：取樣目的應在設計過程中盡早確認並記錄。這是因為取樣點的位置、閥種選擇、管道尺寸和人員可及性必須在 P&ID 和施工圖完成前決定。事後改造既昂貴又困難——這正是許多廠房取樣計畫不合理的根本原因。

法規取樣 vs 製程控制取樣 vs 品質控制取樣

FDA 1993 指南的行動限度仍是工業標準

雖然 USP、EP、JP 的藥典並未規定細菌計數限度，但 FDA 1993 年高純度水檢查指南所訂的限度（PW ≤100 cfu/mL，WFI ≤10 cfu/100 mL）已成為全球製藥廠實際執行的事實標準。在偏差調查和法規審查中，這些數字是基準線。

警戒/行動水準的統計設定實務

設定警戒（Alert）和行動（Action）水準的正確做法：

  1. 收集至少 3–6 個月的歷史穩態數據
  2. 計算均值（μ）和標準差（σ）
  3. 警戒水準 = μ + 2σ；行動水準 = μ + 3σ
  4. 確保行動水準低於藥典規格（留有緩衝空間）

常見錯誤：將行動水準直接設在藥典規格，沒有緩衝。這樣的設定使系統沒有早期預警的機會。

比喻：警戒/行動水準像汽車儀表板

警戒水準（Alert）= 油量警示燈亮起（還有油，但需要注意）
行動水準（Action）= 緊急警告音（需要立即加油）
規格限度（OOS）= 拋錨（已造成問題）
好的系統設計讓你在「拋錨」之前有足夠時間反應。

CDMO 多客戶場景：警戒水準的挑戰

在 CDMO 環境中，同一條水迴路服務不同客戶，但各客戶可能要求不同的警戒/行動水準（部分跨國製藥公司的內部標準比藥典更嚴格）。建議做法：在 CDMO 層級設定最嚴格的統一標準，並在客戶合約中明確記錄合規依據。

Practice Questions | 練習思考

  1. A water system has historical WFI bioburden data with mean 0.5 cfu/100 mL and standard deviation 1.2 cfu/100 mL. Calculate the Alert Level (2σ) and Action Level (3σ). Are these below the FDA 10 cfu/100 mL action limit? （計算警戒和行動水準，並確認是否低於 FDA 限度。）
  2. Alert Level excursions occur at three POUs on the same day, all in the same sub-loop. What does the guide say about concurrent excursions at multiple locations? What is the appropriate next step? （同一子迴路三個 POU 同日超出警戒，下一步應如何？）
  3. Explain why it is inappropriate to monitor conductivity and hardness at the same sampling point (e.g., after a carbon bed). Use the process control purpose rationale. （為何在碳床後同時監測導電率和硬度是不恰當的？）
2.1.2

2.1.2.4–2.1.2.5: Quality Control & Investigative Sampling | 品質控制與調查取樣

Duplicating manufacturing conditions; OOS investigations; diagnostic sampling | 複製製造條件；OOS 調查；診斷取樣

2.1.2.4 Quality Control Purposes

When monitoring for quality control of the water, the intent is to:

  1. Exactly duplicate the quality of water that is being used for manufacturing by collecting samples at routine intervals
  2. Collect water samples at the beginning of a period when the water is being drawn from the system for manufacturing use

Exact duplication of the preparatory procedures utilized by manufacturing should be used during sampling, and should include use of the same:

  • Outlet sanitization practice (if applicable)
  • Hose and gasket
  • Outlet flush procedure (if any)
  • Attached devices such as heat exchangers, reducers, adapters, check valves, and flow meters

The purpose of including all of these potential sources of contamination in the flow path for sampling is to attempt to duplicate the water quality delivered to the manufacturing process, including any heterogeneously distributed contaminants from associated biofilms on or within these components.

Hard-piped or otherwise permanent connections between the water system and manufacturing equipment, as well as automatic valves, create challenges for obtaining samples that duplicate the way water is used by manufacturing. One engineering solution may be to utilize a three-way divert valve that may be installed on the manufacturing equipment.

While POU valves with a built-in upstream sample port may be used when sampling for process control purposes, they are typically not used when sampling for quality control purposes. The only exceptions are:

  • The conduit is routinely sanitized with a validated procedure prior to water use for manufacturing (hot water, steam, or chemicals), so the conduit provides no added contamination
  • There is no feasible engineering solution that allows sampling exactly as used during manufacturing
  • The relevant attributes at that particular POU are not microbial (only homogeneously distributed chemical impurities, e.g., for a washer whose cycle ends with a hot drying step)

2.1.2.5 Sampling for Technical, Investigative, or Diagnostic Reasons

Sampling performed for technical, investigative, or diagnostic reasons may include:

  • Gathering data to better understand or pinpoint the root cause of a process deviation or specification excursion
  • To determine the extent of contamination within a system
  • To spot-check the long-term efficacy of a particular remedial action (e.g., from a CAPA response)

Additional sampling points installed for technical, investigative, or troubleshooting purposes may not be routinely sampled. Data from technical, investigative, or diagnostic sampling can also be used to establish a baseline for non-routinely measured water attributes which may be valuable in future investigations. Samplings of this nature are typically done only occasionally and only when needed for long-term profiling or as part of an investigation.

Alert, Action, and Out Of Specification (OOS) Levels

Sampling could be performed from the same sample location for both process control and quality control purposes. Different Alert and Action Levels could be established; however, process control levels may typically be established at tighter values than those for quality control.

For an excursion above a specification limit, an investigation should be performed to determine, correct, and prevent the cause. The particular investigation would be an OOS investigation and the impact of this water on the product should be assessed.

中文解析：品質控制取樣的嚴格要求

QC 取樣：「模擬製造」的核心要求

品質控制取樣的本質是複製製造行為。這意味著：

  • 用相同的軟管和墊圈
  • 執行相同的出水口消毒程序
  • 保留相同的下游設備（熱交換器、流量計）
  • 在製造開始前取樣（而非取樣後才安裝設備）

直接影響：取樣結果代表的是「進入產品的水質」，而非「迴路中的水質」。

POU 上游取樣埠：QC 取樣的陷阱

許多廠房為了方便，在 POU 閥的上游安裝取樣埠。這對製程控制（PC）取樣是可接受的，但對品質控制（QC）取樣通常不合格——因為上游取樣埠繞過了閥座、軟管、熱交換器等微生物熱點，無法代表實際進入產品的水質。

CDMO 實務：硬接管製造設備的取樣挑戰

現代無菌灌裝設備通常直接硬接管到 WFI 系統，無法拆卸取樣。ISPE 建議的解決方案：

  • 三通轉向閥（three-way divert valve）：在設備入口安裝，允許水流轉向至取樣容器
  • 設備隔離閥旁邊的取樣埠：在水首次流入製造槽時取樣
  • 直接斷開管道（若可行）：將水流引向取樣容器代替流入設備

這些工程解決方案應在廠房設計階段就規劃，而非在驗證時才發現問題。

OOS 調查 vs 趨勢偏差

比喻：調查取樣像犯罪現場鑑識

當常規監控發現異常（如某一 POU 突然出現高菌計數），調查取樣就像犯罪現場鑑識：在問題附近增加取樣點，逐步縮小範圍，找出污染源（可能是某個閥座損壞、某段管道形成死腿）。調查取樣的數據通常不用於常規放行，而是用於根本原因分析。

Practice Questions | 練習思考

  1. A QC technician collects a WFI sample from the upstream port of a POU diaphragm valve (before the hose and heat exchanger). Bioburden result: 0 cfu/100 mL. Can this result be used to release the batch? Why or why not? （從 POU 閥上游取樣的微生物結果可以用於批次放行嗎？）
  2. An OOS WFI result (25 cfu/100 mL) is obtained from a fill-finish room POU. The QC manager wants to resample immediately. What should happen before resampling, according to this guide's OOS investigation framework? （在重新取樣之前，根據 ISPE 的 OOS 調查框架應先做什麼？）
  3. Your CDMO site is launching a new injectable product with a dedicated formulation room. The WFI drop to the formulation vessel is permanently piped. Describe the sampling strategy you would implement, specifying valve type and sampling procedure. （為新的注射劑配製室設計 WFI 取樣策略，說明閥型和取樣程序。）
2.2

2.2 Determining Sampling Locations | 確定取樣位置

Risk-based approach; loop geometry; critical points; microbiological hot spots | 風險評估；迴路幾何；關鍵點；微生物熱點

2.2 Determining Sampling Locations

Locating sample points to ensure samples are taken from suitable process locations before and after unit operations, at points of use and elsewhere, should assure a successful water system monitoring program.

A Risk Analysis (RA) may be performed to help determine sample locations. The RA can provide a rationale for the sampling points in a water system and can help to define the intended purpose of each sampling location, based on established CQAs and Critical Process Parameters (CPPs).

Sample valve locations should be addressed not only on a P&ID but should also be addressed during equipment and piping installation. Components, hardware, or other items that interfere with correct sampling techniques should be avoided through careful planning and appropriate field execution. Considerations should include the disposition of waste from flushing, location of sample ports relative to other equipment, local environmental issues, and other concerns. Design in consultation with QA, QC, and Microbiology Subject Matter Experts (SMEs) is desirable.

"Sample valves located in return loop piping that are inaccessible to samplers, sample valves blocked by other equipment or with otherwise limited access... do not accomplish the goal of ensuring that the samples are representative. Improper location may put a sampler's safety at risk or may yield data with a high degree of variability, and may result in an increase in alert limit, action limit, and OOS findings."

Sampling locations should include all appropriate sections of the system including:

  • Source water
  • Pretreatment unit operations
  • Primary and final treatment
  • Storage
  • Distribution systems (main loops and sub loops)
  • POU and any special POU treatments

Text-Based Loop Diagram: Typical PW/WFI Distribution System

PURIFIED WATER / WFI DISTRIBUTION LOOP ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────── [TANK] ──→ [PUMP] ──→ SUPPLY HEADER │ ┌────────────────────────┼──────────────────────┐ │ │ │ [POU-1] [POU-2] [POU-3] Room 101 Room 102 Room 103 (1st POU) (Mid-loop POU) (Last POU) │ │ │ └────────────────────────┼──────────────────────┘ │ RETURN HEADER ──→ [TANK] SAMPLING STRATEGY: ★ = Mandatory sample point ★ Supply (after pump, before 1st POU) Purpose: PC — confirm generation system output quality ★ POU-1 (1st Point of Use) Purpose: QC — first use point, baseline for loop ★ POU-2 (Representative mid-loop POU) Purpose: QC — mid-loop check ★ POU-3 (Last Point of Use) Purpose: QC — worst-case for temperature drop / flow ↑ Most remote from supply = highest microbial risk ★ Return (after last POU, before tank) Purpose: PC — cumulative loop performance ↑ Worst-case for chemical quality DEADLEG RISK ZONES (▲ = high risk): ▲ Any side branch with valve closed long-term ▲ POU valve seat (wet/moist surface) ▲ Hose connection points ▲ Heat exchanger water-side (if temperature drops) ▲ Overnight stagnation in any non-circulating branch

Figure: Simplified PW/WFI distribution loop showing mandatory sampling locations and microbial risk zones. Actual systems require sampling at ALL POUs for QC purposes.

中文解析：取樣位置選擇的風險評估方法

風險分析（RA）在取樣點選擇中的角色

ISPE 建議在廠房設計的概念階段（Conceptual Design）就進行取樣位置的風險分析。RA 應回答以下問題：

  • 哪些位置的水質失控會直接影響產品 CQA？（優先取樣）
  • 哪些位置可以用在線儀表替代手動取樣？（均質雜質）
  • 哪些位置存在特殊的微生物或化學污染風險？（熱點）
  • 人員能否安全、方便地在該位置取樣？（可及性）

迴路幾何與取樣策略的關聯

WFI/PW 迴路的幾何設計直接決定取樣策略：

關鍵警告：取樣點可及性影響數據品質

ISPE 直接指出：取樣點不可及會導致警戒/行動水準超出次數增加——因為人員在困難條件下取樣容易引入外部污染，造成假陽性。常見的可及性問題：

  • 回流管道安裝在天花板或管道夾層中
  • 取樣點被其他設備遮擋
  • 取樣點高度超過 1.8 公尺，需要梯子
  • 取樣廢水無法安全排放（直接滴在地板上）

比喻：迴路設計像城市地鐵規劃

WFI 迴路就像地鐵環線：每個站（POU）都需要監控，但終點站（最後一個 POU 和回流口）是最重要的——乘客（水分子）在整條線上累積了所有可能的污染。同樣道理，回流口的水質代表整條迴路的「最差情況」，是製程控制監控的首選位置。

Practice Questions | 練習思考

  1. A WFI loop has 8 POUs, with POU-7 located 80 meters from the supply header and POU-8 only 5 meters from the return header. Which POU poses the highest microbial risk and why? Where should you install a process control sampling point? （哪個 POU 微生物風險最高？製程控制取樣點應設在哪裡？）
  2. During design review, a validation engineer notices that all three return-loop sample valves are installed in a pipe rack 2.4 meters above the floor, accessible only by a ladder. What risks does ISPE warn about? What design change would you recommend? （回流管道取樣點安裝在 2.4 公尺高處，有什麼風險？建議如何改進？）
  3. Your CDMO is adding a new sub-loop to serve a new suite. The sub-loop returns to the main loop return header. Where must you install a sample point, and what is its purpose? （新增子迴路連接主回流管，取樣點應設在哪裡？）
2.2.1

2.2.1–2.2.3: Source Water, Pretreatment & Primary Treatment | 水源、前處理與初步處理

Potable feed water requirements; unit operation monitoring; before/after sampling strategy | 飲用水標準；單元操作監控；前後取樣策略

2.2.1 Source Water

Source water feeding any compendial pharmaceutical water system should meet local drinking water standards such as those specified by the WHO, the US Environmental Protection Agency (EPA), drinking water regulations of the EU or Japan, or other competent authorities.

Source water that does not meet potable or drinking water standards should be brought into compliance with recognized drinking water regulations prior to being used to feed a pharmaceutical water system.

Chlorination (or chloramination) of municipal water has become common in many areas of the world for microbiological control. If residual chlorine levels are inadequate for microbial control, rechlorination may be required and should be defined in a SOP and monitored on a regular basis through an appropriately located sample port.

Complete chemical analysis of source water that confirms it meets the appropriate potable or drinking water requirements may be performed on a periodic basis to trend incoming contaminant levels and to make system adjustments if required. If a source water storage tank is employed, additional testing after storage is advisable before water enters the water purification system.

2.2.2 Pretreatment Unit Operations

Sampling locations should be included before and after each unit operation for diagnostic purposes so that monitoring can be performed as required. Sampling before and after individual unit operations helps in establishing a unit operation's performance.

The following unit operations are examples of monitoring locations that may be considered:

  • Before and after media filtration (multi-media, cartridge, etc.)
  • Before and after softeners
  • Before and after Activated Carbon Filters (microbial monitoring is additionally critical here because activated carbon beds tend to promote microbial growth)
  • Before and after Ultraviolet units
  • Before and after chlorination or dechlorination units
  • Before and after Reverse Osmosis (RO), Continuous Electro Deionization (CEDI), or ion exchange units
  • Before and after any other unit operations within the pretreatment system boundary

2.2.3 Primary and Final Treatment

Primary and final treatment for compendial or non-compendial water may include several different treatment technologies. Examples include:

  • Reverse osmosis
  • Continuous electro deionization (CEDI)
  • Ion exchange deionization
  • Microfiltration / Ultrafiltration / Nanofiltration
  • Distillation (still for WFI)
  • Ultraviolet treatment
  • Heat exchangers

Sampling locations should be provided before and after each treatment unit operation as appropriate. Attributes to be evaluated are based on equipment performance expectations and may include: Conductivity, TOC, Chlorine, Ammonia, Hardness, Silica, Silt Density Index (SDI), Microbial, and Endotoxin.

Final treatment unit output water should be monitored using in-line, on-line or at-line analyzers where possible. Conductivity and TOC analyzers are usually used for these purposes. Where multiple final treatment units are present in a facility, there should be a sample point before and after each.

中文解析：從水源到純化系統的取樣邏輯

水源水質的重要性

純化水和注射用水系統的性能高度依賴進水水質。進水水質的季節性變化（如雨季帶入更多有機物、夏季氯化加重）會影響下游設備的負荷和性能。建議：

  • 每季對水源進行全項化學分析
  • 監測氯殘留量（目標：0.2–0.5 mg/L）
  • 建立進水水質的趨勢分析，作為純化系統預防性維護的觸發依據

活性碳過濾器：微生物監控的特別關注點

ISPE 特別指出活性碳床（Activated Carbon Filter）會促進微生物生長——這是反直覺的！活性碳雖然能去除氯（脫氯），但脫氯後的水失去了抑菌作用，加上碳床表面積巨大，是理想的生物膜生長環境。

實務建議：活性碳床後的微生物取樣頻率應比其他前處理設備高；部分廠商選擇用臭氧或 UV 替代活性碳，以減少微生物風險。

前後取樣的診斷價值

在每個單元操作「前後」取樣的目的是建立各設備的性能基準（performance baseline）。

實例：RO 前後的電導率差異反映 RO 膜的去除效率（rejection rate）。若某次 RO 後電導率高於正常值，前後取樣數據可立即判斷是否為膜損壞所致（前後差異縮小），而非進水水質問題（前後差異比例不變）。

CDMO 挑戰：多套純化設備的取樣點數量

大型 CDMO 廠可能有 2–3 套 PW 純化系統和 2 套 WFI 蒸餾器，共用多個儲槽和配水迴路。取樣點數量可能超過 50 個。管理策略：

  • 以在線儀表（TOC、導電率）覆蓋均質屬性
  • 僅在最高風險點保留手動取樣（碳床後、蒸餾器後、配水迴路回流）
  • 以 LIMS 系統管理取樣排程和趨勢分析

Practice Questions | 練習思考

  1. A PW system uses: multimedia filter → softener → activated carbon filter → RO → CEDI. List all the sampling locations you would install and identify the primary attribute(s) to monitor at each. （列出所有取樣位置和各點的主要監控屬性。）
  2. Source water chlorine levels drop from 0.4 mg/L to 0.05 mg/L due to a municipal supply change. What impact might this have downstream, and what sampling action would you trigger? （進水餘氯從 0.4 降至 0.05 mg/L，下游可能有什麼影響？）
  3. Your WFI still produces water that passes conductivity but fails endotoxin (3.0 EU/mL vs. limit 0.25 EU/mL). Using before/after sampling logic, which equipment would you test first to locate the source? （WFI 蒸餾水導電率合格但內毒素超標，用前後取樣邏輯如何追溯污染源？）
2.2.4

2.2.4–2.2.6: Storage Tanks, Distribution Systems & Points of Use | 儲槽、配水系統與使用點

Tank sampling strategy; loop return worst-case; POU definition and sampling requirements | 儲槽取樣；迴路回流最差情況；POU 定義

2.2.4 Storage Tanks

Sampling locations directly on a storage tank may provide valuable information if any microbial buildup (biofilm) is occurring in the tank and also allows testing of the stored water quality. A sample valve installed for direct sampling from the storage tank may be required for validation or for diagnostic purposes and may or may not be used for routine sampling.

Sampling valves located at storage tanks should be easily accessible and should minimize the risk of contamination of the sample and also the storage tank itself during sampling.

Tank water quality can also be assessed indirectly through monitoring of:

  • The primary generation supply (incoming water to storage)
  • The loop return (water returning to storage)
  • The tank outlet which feeds the pumps and subsequently the use points

These samples indicate the water quality prior to entry to the storage tank, after returning from the loop, and at the storage tank outlet, providing an indirect indication of the impact the storage tank is having on water quality.

2.2.5 Distribution Systems (main loops and sub loops)

Quality control sampling locations in the main distribution system should include all POUs, with sampling occurring in a manner identical to how the water is used by manufacturing. Process control sampling locations should be located before the first and after the last POU and at other specified locations.

Sampling the loop return after the last POU ensures process control as this location may be the worst case location for water quality in the entire distribution system. Water systems with multiple return loops should have sampling locations in each of the return loops. For one-way (non-recirculating) branch systems, all POUs should be sampled.

When temperature changes are required, the distribution system should be designed such that the pharmaceutical water is maintained at a higher pressure than heating/cooling media such as in a heat exchanger to prevent leakage from the non-sanitary utility to the sanitary side of the heat exchanger.

Each sub-loop returning to the main loop return should have a sampling point before the sub loop connects to the main loop return.

In the distribution loop of a pharmaceutical water system, all use point valves and sample valves should be of a sanitary design. Sample points in a laboratory system may not be sanitary and may contain dead legs such as may be present in a gooseneck faucet.

2.2.6 Points of Use

A Point Of Use (POU) is defined as the location where the water delivered from the water distribution system is actually used. POUs may be located on the main loop or in sub loops.

When sampling for quality control purposes, the POU is typically not the valve on the distribution system itself from which the water is taken. Instead, it is the end of the delivery system that transfers the water from the distribution system to the process (e.g., sinks, autoclaves, washers, process tanks). Sampling at POUs should include all components and surfaces along this water delivery pathway (e.g., heat exchangers, hoses, fittings) that the water needs to travel through to reach the process.

When the outlet of a POU cannot be sampled, the next most representative sampling location should be identified. Rationale for the selection should be provided in the risk assessment. Validation and/or routine monitoring data should conclude that the sample location is representative of the POU.

Every POU in a water distribution system that is not active should be locked out or tagged out of service and should be appropriately maintained to prevent contamination of the POU or the distribution system.

中文解析：儲槽、配水迴路與 POU 的取樣策略

儲槽取樣：直接 vs 間接評估

直接在儲槽上設取樣點（如槽側壁上的取樣閥）可以評估槽內生物膜狀況，但實際操作中風險較高（取樣時可能污染儲槽）。更常見且風險較低的替代方案是：通過監測入水、回流水和出水三個位置的水質，間接推斷儲槽對水質的影響。

迴路回流口：最差情況（Worst Case）的含義

「回流口是整個配水系統水質最差的位置」這一結論的邏輯：

  • 水從儲槽出發，流過整條迴路，最後從回流口返回
  • 沿途每個 POU、每個閥、每個管接頭都有機會引入微生物
  • 水在迴路中行走最長距離，累積了所有潛在污染

因此，回流口的製程控制取樣代表迴路整體狀況的最保守評估。如果回流口水質合格，迴路中間點幾乎必然合格（但 POU 因為有延伸管路，仍需獨立取樣）。

POU 的正確定義：延伸管路的重要性

ISPE 對 POU 的定義容易被誤解。POU 不是配水系統上的閥門，而是「水實際被使用的末端位置」。

舉例：一個 WFI 閥後連接一段軟管，軟管連接一個熱交換器，最後進入配製槽。在這個案例中：

  • POU = 配製槽入口（水實際使用的地方）
  • QC 取樣點 = 盡可能接近配製槽入口，包含軟管和熱交換器
  • PC 取樣點可以在 WFI 閥的上游取樣埠

CDMO 實務：停用 POU 的管理

在 CDMO 環境中，隨著客戶產品的變化，某些 POU 可能長期停用（如某條生產線停產）。ISPE 要求停用的 POU 必須 lock out / tag out 並妥善維護。實務上的最佳做法：

  • 在 SOP 中定義停用 POU 的管理流程（關閉、排水、隔離）
  • 停用的支管應定期沖洗（如每週）或完全隔離拆除
  • 恢復使用前，必須先進行微生物和化學取樣確認

熱交換器的壓差管理

當配水系統中包含熱交換器（如溫度調節）時，ISPE 要求藥用水側的壓力應高於加熱/冷卻介質側，以防止非衛生側的冷凝水或冷卻水滲入藥用水。若無法確保壓差，應使用雙管板熱交換器（double tube sheet），並監測下游導電率/TOC 作為洩漏指標。

Practice Questions | 練習思考

  1. A WFI loop return sample consistently shows bioburden of 8 cfu/100 mL (Action Limit: 10 cfu/100 mL). Individual POU results are all <1 cfu/100 mL. What does this pattern suggest about where the contamination is coming from? （回流口菌計數接近行動水準但各 POU 均低，這說明污染源在哪裡？）
  2. A formulation POU connects to the WFI loop with: POU valve → 2m hose → 0.2 µm filter → formulation vessel. For a QC microbial sample, should you sample before or after the filter? What does ISPE say about sampling "as used"? （取樣點應在 0.2 µm 過濾器前還是後？ISPE 的「以使用方式取樣」原則如何應用？）
  3. A production line POU has been inactive for 3 months (locked out). Manufacturing wants to restart it next week. What sampling protocol would you require before allowing it to be used for product contact water? （停用 3 個月的 POU 重新啟用前，需要執行哪些取樣確認？）

Key Takeaways: Sections 2.1–2.2

  • Water is used in 5 roles; sampling must mirror the actual use condition
  • Chemical (homogeneous) impurities can be monitored with validated online instruments at the loop return; microbiological (heterogeneous) attributes require per-POU sampling
  • 99.9%+ of bacteria reside in biofilm; planktonic counts are lagging indicators
  • Five purposes of sampling: regulatory, consensus, process control, quality control, investigative — each requires different location and frequency logic
  • Alert Levels = 2σ; Action Levels = 3σ — both must be below specification to allow time for remediation
  • QC sampling must include all downstream components (hoses, heat exchangers) to be representative
  • Loop return = worst-case for PC; most-remote POU = worst-case for microbial risk
  • Each sub-loop must have its own sample point before rejoining the main return
  • Inactive POUs must be locked/tagged out; pre-use sampling required before restarting
中文總結：本節核心要點
  • 水的五種角色 → 取樣方式必須模擬實際使用條件
  • 化學（均質）雜質：可以用迴路回流口在線儀表替代 POU 手動取樣；微生物（非均質）雜質：必須每個 POU 手動取樣
  • 系統中 99.9% 以上的細菌存在於生物膜中；浮游菌計數是滯後指標
  • 取樣目的的五大類別：法規、共識標準、製程控制、品質控制、技術調查
  • 警戒水準 = μ+2σ；行動水準 = μ+3σ；兩者均必須低於藥典規格，留有緩衝
  • 品質控制取樣必須包含下游所有組件（軟管、熱交換器）才具代表性
  • 迴路回流口 = 製程控制最差情況；最遠端 POU = 微生物風險最高點
  • 每個子迴路在匯入主回流前必須設獨立取樣點
  • 停用 POU 必須 lock out/tag out；重新啟用前需執行取樣確認

CDMO 行動清單

  • 在廠房設計的概念/詳細設計階段進行水取樣點的 RA
  • P&ID 中標注所有取樣點，並在現場確認可及性和廢水排放
  • 建立以使用方式為基礎的 QC 取樣 SOP，包含軟管、熱交換器等所有下游組件
  • 以 3–6 個月穩態數據統計設定 Alert/Action 水準
  • 在 LIMS 中建立趨勢警報，自動偵測多點同時超出警戒水準的情況
  • 制定停用 POU 管理程序，含重新啟用前的取樣要求

製藥用水：取樣計畫（確效框架） | p24-p38

Chapter 2 Part 2: Pharmaceutical Water — Sampling Plans Framework

製藥用水：取樣計畫框架 | Sections 2.3.1 – 2.3.5.4
ISPE Good Practice Guide (2016): Sampling for Pharmaceutical Water, Steam, and Process Gases  |  pp. 25–31

Learning Objectives  |  學習目標

  • Describe the three phases of Performance Qualification (PQ) sampling and their durations
  • Distinguish between chemical attribute sampling and microbiological sampling frequency rationale
  • Identify worst case conditions that must be addressed in a PQ sampling plan
  • Explain the regulatory basis for sampling frequency across USP, EP, JP, and ICH Q7
  • Define alert levels vs. action levels and their application to water systems
  • Apply risk-based thinking to pretreatment, PW, and WFI sampling design
  • Recognize special scenarios (power failure, maintenance events) requiring validation
  • 描述性能確認（PQ）取樣的三個階段及各階段持續時間
  • 區分化學屬性取樣與微生物取樣頻率的設計邏輯
  • 識別PQ取樣計畫中必須涵蓋的最壞情況條件
  • 解釋USP、EP、JP及ICH Q7對取樣頻率的法規依據
  • 定義警戒水準與行動水準，並應用於水系統監控
  • 將基於風險的思維應用於前處理、PW及WFI取樣設計
  • 識別需要確認的特殊情境（停電、維護事件）
